The airplane Biden taxied past, with tail number 10015, isnâ€™t one of the planes used as Air Force One.  Itâ€™s a smaller Boeing C40-B (military version of 737-700) operated by the Air Force for VIP transport.  AF1 is usually a Boeing VC-25 (military version of 747-200B) with tail number 28000 or 29000 (2 identical planes).  Whatever airplane the President is on is Air Force One, but the plane takes on its tail designation whenever the President is not on board.  Similar for AF2 and the Vice President.  VP Harris will typically fly on a Boeing C-32 (military 757-200), with the tail number 80002, which will be its designation when she is not aboard.

1:39 minor note: While any plane is "Air Force One" when the President is on it, the plane we saw in that is a Boeing C-40, which is almost never Air Force One. Most presidents use either the C-32 (Boeing 757) or VC-25 (Boeing 747) as Air Force One.
